 2620 |  1  tkdemo.s   1895 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | ************************************************************
 2621 |  1  tkdemo.s   1896 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | *
 2622 |  1  tkdemo.s   1897 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * Many of the tool kit calls require that the mouse
 2623 |  1  tkdemo.s   1898 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * coordinates be passed back to the tool kit. Since
 2624 |  1  tkdemo.s   1899 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * the mouse coordinates are originally provided in
 2625 |  1  tkdemo.s   1900 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * the event parameters, using the same memory to pass
 2626 |  1  tkdemo.s   1901 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * parameters to the tool kit saves us the trouble of
 2627 |  1  tkdemo.s   1902 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * moving the information around.
 2628 |  1  tkdemo.s   1903 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | *
 2629 |  1  tkdemo.s   1904 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * Below I equate many labels to the same memory. When
 2630 |  1  tkdemo.s   1905 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * I use them in the code I try to indicate (in a comment
 2631 |  1  tkdemo.s   1906 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * that they refer to this shared area).
 2632 |  1  tkdemo.s   1907 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | *
 2633 |  1  tkdemo.s   1908 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | *
 2634 |  1  tkdemo.s   1909 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * The event parameter is five bytes long. The first byte
 2635 |  1  tkdemo.s   1910 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * is the event type.  The remaining bytes depend on the
 2636 |  1  tkdemo.s   1911 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/16E0               | * value of the first byte.
